WHAT IT SHOWS: your live Bluesky followers in big readable numbers, plus posts and following, a next-milestone progress bar toward 1K, 10K, 100K, and a "+N today" ticker. Refreshes every minute over Wi-Fi.  IN THE BOX: A pre-flashed Social Meter, USB-C cable, desk stand, and a setup card. Setup takes about two minutes from your phone.  WHAT YOU NEED: Your Bluesky handle - no API key required. Plus 2.4 GHz home Wi-Fi (WPA2).  * Social Meter is an independent hardware project. WHAT IT SHOWS: your live Mastodon followers in big readable numbers, plus posts and following, a next-milestone progress bar toward 1K, 10K, 100K, and a "+N today" ticker. Refreshes every minute over Wi-Fi.  IN THE BOX: A pre-flashed Social Meter, USB-C cable, desk stand, and a setup card. Setup takes about two minutes from your phone.  WHAT YOU NEED: Your full handle (user@instance) - no API key required. Plus 2.4 GHz home Wi-Fi (WPA2).  * Social Meter is an independent hardware project. WHAT IT SHOWS: your live Etsy shop sales in big readable numbers, plus admirers and reviews, a next-milestone progress bar toward 100, 1K, 10K, and a "+N today" ticker. Refreshes every minute over Wi-Fi.  IN THE BOX: A pre-flashed Social Meter, USB-C cable, desk stand, and a setup card. Setup takes about two minutes from your phone.  WHAT YOU NEED: Your Etsy shop name; A free Etsy key - keystring:shared_secret joined by a colon (from developers.etsy.com). Plus 2.4 GHz home Wi-Fi (WPA2).  * Social Meter is an independent hardware project.
